# <a name="release-notes-for-current-channel"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-103">有关当前频道的发行说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-103">Release notes for Current Channel</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-104">我们为 Microsoft 365 企业应用版、Microsoft 365 商业应用版以及 Project 和 Visio 桌面应用的订阅版本提供了当前频道更新。这些发行说明提供了有关这些更新中所含新功能和非安全更新的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-104">These release notes provide information about new features and non-security updates that are included in Current Channel updates for Microsoft 365 Apps for enterprise, Microsoft 365 Apps for business, and the subscription versions of the desktop apps for Project and Visio.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-105">我们正在对 Microsoft 365 应用的更新频道进行一些更改，包括添加新的更新频道（月度企业版频道）和更改现有更新频道的名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-105">We’re making some changes to the update channels for Microsoft 365 Apps, including adding a new update channel (Monthly Enterprise Channel) and changing the names of the existing update channels.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-106">若要了解详细信息，请[阅读这篇文章](/DeployOffice/update-channels-changes)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-106">To learn more, [read this article](/DeployOffice/update-channels-changes).</span></span>

 > [!NOTE]
>
>- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-107">我们经常会过一段时间就将功能（有时甚至是修补程序）发布到当前频道更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-107">We often roll out features (and sometimes even fixes) to Current over a period of time.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-108">如果没有立即看到下述内容，则很快就会看到的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-108">If you don’t see something described below right away, you can expect it soon.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-109">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-109">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/when-do-i-get-the-newest-features-in-for-office-365-da36192c-58b9-4bc9-8d51-bb6eed468516)
>- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-110">Microsoft Teams 的功能可能不同于最新发布的当前频道，因为前者具有更高的发布频率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-110">Microsoft Teams features may differ from the latest Current Channel released as they have a more frequent release cadence.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-116">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-116">Resolved issues</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-119">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-119">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-120">我们修复了导致 Outlook 替代 OWA 中配置的重点收件箱首选项这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-120">We fixed an issue that caused Outlook to override the Focused Inbox preferences configured in OWA.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-121">我们修复了一个问题，该问题导致当代表另一个用户发送邮件，并针对不是全局地址列表的通讯簿进行解析时，名称解析失败。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-121">We fixed an issue that caused name resolution to fail when sending on behalf of another user and resolving against an address book that is not the Global Address List.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-124">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-124">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-136">我们解决了导致代理人显示为新添加的日历上创建的会议的组织者这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-136">We fixed an issue that caused delegates to appear as the organizer of meetings created on newly added calendars.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-137">在此州/省/市/区中的会议不会在主体的日历上显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-137">Meetings in this state did not appear on the principal's calendar.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-151">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-151">Resolved issues</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-153">修复了具有 ARM 处理器的计算机上，启用 MAPI 的应用程序所使用的 Outlook 组件中的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-153">We fixed an issue in a component of Outlook that is used by MAPI-enabled applications on computers with ARM processors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-154">该问题导致搜索失败，或因背景应用重复重新启动导致计算机的额外负载。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-154">The issue was causing search to fail or causing extra load on the computer as background apps restarted repeatedly.</span></span>

## <a name="version-2103-march-30"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-155">版本 2103：3 月 30 日</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-155">Version 2103: March 30</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-156">*版本 2103（内部版本 13901.20312）*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-156">*Version 2103 (Build 13901.20312)*</span></span>

[//]: # (请勿移除功能详细信息内容开头)

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-158">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-158">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-159">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-159">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-160">**撰写邮件时节省时间：** Outlook 显示编写建议，可帮助你快速撰写邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-160">**Save time while composing messages:** Outlook shows you writing suggestions that help you compose messages quickly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-161">若要接受建议，只需使用 Tab 键。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-161">To accept the suggestion, just use the Tab key.</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-162">在[博客文章](https://insider.office.com/zh-CN/blog/text-predictions-in-word-outlook)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-162">See details in [blog post](https://insider.office.com/zh-CN/blog/text-predictions-in-word-outlook)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-163">**新式会议室和工作区预定体验：** 会议室预定体验已刷新，通过此体验，我们添加了允许你安排个别工作区的功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-163">**New conference room and workspace booking experience:** The conference room booking experience has been refreshed, and with it we've added capabilities to allow you to schedule individual workspaces as well</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-164">**选择搜索位置：**“新建搜索范围”下拉列表使你能够更轻松地修改搜索并在当前文件夹和当前邮箱之间切换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-164">**Pick where to search:** The new search scope drop down allows you to more easily modify your search and switch between Current Folder and Current Mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-165">感谢在“即将推出”中对新的“热门搜索”体验提供反馈的每个人员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-165">Thank you to everyone in Coming Soon who provided feedback on the new Search at Top experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-166">此项设计和更新正是来自于该反馈！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-166">This design and update came out of that feedback!</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-167">**搜索人员时获取会议建议：** 在搜索框中键入人员姓名时，搜索建议中将包含日历邀请的最相关电子邮件包括在内。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-167">**Get meeting suggestions when you search for a person:** When you type a person’s name in the Search box, the most relevant email containing calendar invites will be included with your search suggestions.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-168">**共享到 Teams：** 与 Teams 中的人员或频道共享 Outlook 中的邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-168">**Share to Teams:** Share messages from Outlook with a person or channel in Teams.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-169">**使用语音撰写邮件：** 使用新的听写工具栏，语音命令，自动标点符号等撰写邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-169">**Draft messages with your voice:** Use the new dictation toolbar, voice commands, auto-punctuation, and more to compose messages.</span></span>

### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-170">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-170">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-171">**会议反应：** 会议反应是在会议中进行交互的新方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-171">**Meeting Reactions:** Meeting reactions are a new way to interact in meetings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-172">参与者可以发送反应，并且这些反应将以流的形式显示在共享内容以及发送响应的个人上（如果它们在会议阶段显示）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-172">Participants can send reactions and they'll be shown as a stream on content that is shared, and on the individual who sent the reaction if they're displayed on the meeting stage.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-173">**在 Teams 会议中管理与会者音频权限的改进：** 会议演示者和组织者现可允许与会者取消静音，即使不上手。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-173">**Improvement for managing attendee audio permissions in a Teams Meeting:** Meeting presenters and organizers can now allow attendees to unmute even if their hand isn't raised.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-174">以前，阻止取消静音（已禁用麦克风）的会议与会者必须抬起手来允许取消静音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-174">Previously, meeting attendees that were prevented from unmuting (mic disabled) had to raise their hand to be allowed to unmute.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-175">**在 Teams 会议中管理与会者音频权限的改进：** 以前，会议演示者或组织者无法禁用会议中单个与会者的麦克风。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-175">**Improvement for managing attendee audio permissions in a Teams Meeting:** Previously, meeting presenters or organizers couldn't disable the mic of a single attendee in a meeting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-176">组织者或演示者只能将"允许与会者取消静音"设置为关闭，从而禁用每个与会者的麦克风。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-176">The organizer or presenter could only set "Allow attendees to unmute" to off, thereby disabling the mics of every attendee.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-177">通过此更改，会议演示者和组织者可以防止在工作组会议期间单个与会者以临时方式取消静音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-177">With this change, meeting presenters and organizers can prevent individual attendees from unmuting in an ad-hoc manner during a Teams Meeting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-178">**改进了会议参与者名单的体验：** 现在，我们正在更改参与者列表在"车队"（在会议、演示者和与会者参与者）的 Teams 会议中的显示方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-178">**Improved Experience in the Meeting Participant Roster:** We are now changing how the participant list is displayed in a Teams meeting for the Lobby, In meeting, Presenters, and Attendees participant sections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-179">初始视图中每个节最多显示 20 位参与者，可选择深入研究并查看该分区内的其他参与者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-179">A maximum of 20 participants for each of the sections will be displayed in the initial view, with an option to drill in and view more participants within that section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-180">对于查阅人，可在将全部插入会议之前查看完整列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-180">For the lobby, you can review the full list before you admit all into the meeting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-181">名单将显示会议中大多数活跃参与者的详细信息（按字母顺序排列）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-181">The roster will display details of most active participants in the meeting arranged in alphabetical order.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-182">参与者操作菜单未发生变化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-182">There are no changes to the participants action menu.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-183">**从名单搜索会议参与者：** 从名单中的搜索框搜索，现在用户可以在会议参与者中搜索，以确定是否有特定人员已加入会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-183">**Search meeting participants from the roster:** From the search box in the roster, users can now search currently in the meeting participants, to know whether a particular individual has joined the meeting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-184">他们可继续搜索会议外部参与者，并请求其加入会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-184">They can continue to search for participants outside the meeting and request them to join the meeting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-185">**从 Outlook 共享到 Teams：** Outlook 共享给 Teams 允许你将电子邮件或对话（包括附件）的副本发送到 Teams 聊天和频道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-185">**Share to Teams from Outlook:** Share to Teams from Outlook allows you to send a copy of email messages or conversations, including attachments, into Teams chats and channels.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-186">在 Outlook 功能区或电子邮件的操作菜单上查找"共享到 Teams"选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-186">Find the Share to Teams option in the Outlook ribbon or the action menu for an email.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-187">共享到 Teams 支持 Outlook 网页版、Outlook for Windows 和新的 Outlook for Mac 预览版。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-187">Share to Teams supports Outlook on the web, Outlook for Windows, and the new Outlook for Mac Preview.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-188">**分会议室计时器和会议室分配保留：** 组织者现可通过会议室设置为分会会议室设置计时器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-188">**Breakout Room Timer and Room assignment retention:** Organizers can now set a timer for Breakout rooms from the Breakout Room settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-189">计时器过期后，会议室将自动关闭，且参与者将返回主会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-189">After timer has expired, rooms will automatically close and participants will come back to the main meeting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-190">通过会议室作业保留，可保持多个会话中的会议室配置和分配。使用参与者重新分配功能，组织者现能够在打开会议室时在会议室和主会议间移动加入的参与者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-190">Room assignment retention provides the ability to persist room configuration and assignment over multiple sessions.With participant reassignment capability, organizer will now be able to move joined participants across rooms and main meeting also when rooms are opened.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-191">**脱机访问文件：** 用户现可以访问以前打开的文件，即使没有 Internet 连接也是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-191">**Offline access for files:** Users can now access previously opened files even when there is no internet connectivity.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-192">**共享 PowerPoint 文件时的网格视图：** 在会议上共享 PowerPoint 文件时，用户现在可以使用网格视图查看幻灯片组内的所有幻灯片，以便进行简单的临时幻灯片导航。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-192">**Grid View when sharing a PowerPoint File:** When sharing a PowerPoint file in a meeting, users can now use grid view to see all the slides in the deck for easy ad-hoc slide navigation.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-193">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-193">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-194">**使用语音撰写文档：** 使用新的听写工具栏，语音命令和自动标点来起草文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-194">**Draft documents with your voice:** Use the new dictation toolbar, voice commands and auto-punctuation to draft documents.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-259">**同时取消隐藏多张工作表：** 不再需要一次取消隐藏一个工作表，可以一次取消隐藏多个隐藏工作表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-259">**Unhide many sheets at the same time:** No need to unhide one sheet at a time anymore -- unhide multiple hidden sheets at once.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-260">了解详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-260">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/69f2701a-21f5-4186-87d7-341a8cf53344)

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-261">**改进了条件格式对话框：** 条件格式对话框现在可以调整大小，现在只需单击一下即可复制规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-261">**Improved Conditional Formatting dialogs:** Conditional Formatting dialogs are now resizable, and now you can duplicate the rule with a single click.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-262">了解详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-262">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/fed60dfa-1d3f-4e13-9ecb-f1951ff89d7f)

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-264">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-264">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-265">**更新联系人列表视图：** 联系人列表现在显示电子邮件地址以及更新的照片和文字大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-265">**Updated Contacts list view:** Contacts list now shows email addresses and updated photo and text size.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-266">**使用内置翻译工具打破语言障碍：** 不再需要翻译加载项！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-266">**Break the language barrier with a built-in translator:** Add-ins for translation aren't required anymore!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-267">现可在 Outlook 中使用智能翻译工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-267">You can now use the Intelligent Translator in Outlook.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-268">当你收到一封其他语言的邮件时，邮件顶部将显示一条提示，询问你是否希望 Outlook 将其翻译成默认语言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-268">When you receive a message in another language, a prompt will appear on top of the message asking if you’d like Outlook to translate it to your default language.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-269">也可以右键单击以翻译特定字词、短语或整封邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-269">You can also right-click to translate specific words, phrases, or the whole message.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-270">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-270">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/287380e4-a56c-48a1-9977-f2dca89ce93f)

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-272">**要求用户应用敏感度标签：** 如果组织的策略要求，系统会提示用户应用敏感度标签。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-272">**Require users to apply sensitivity labels:** Users will be prompted to apply a sensitivity label if their organization's policy requires it.</span></span>

### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-273">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-273">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-274">**共享 PowerPoint 文件时的演示者视图：** 在会议中共享 PowerPoint 文件时，演示者现在可以在幻灯片组的所有幻灯片的缩略图条中轻松临时浏览幻灯片。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-274">**Presenter View when sharing a PowerPoint file:** When sharing a PowerPoint file in a meeting, the presenter can now a thumbnail strip of all the slides in the deck for easy ad-hoc slide navigation.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-275">**主题和图标更新：** 我们对默认和深色主题颜色以及图标进行了更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-275">**Theming and icon updates:** We have made updates to the default and dark theme colors and to the icon.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-276">**iPad 上的实时事件演示者支持：** 可以从支持的 iPad 设备上进行实时事件的演示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-276">**Live Event Presenter Support on iPad:** You can present in a live event from your supported iPad device.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-277">**使用 Microsoft Forms 的投票会议参加者：** Teams 会议投票是一种易于发现且无缝的体验，可帮助你召开更具吸引力和高效的会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-277">**Poll meeting participants using Microsoft Forms:** Polls for Teams meetings is an easily discoverable and seamless experience that will help you conduct more engaging and productive meetings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-278">使用由 Microsoft Forms 提供支持的投票，会议演示者可以在会议之前、期间和之后分别在 Teams 会议选项卡下的一个位置准备、发起和评估投票。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-278">With Polls, which is powered by Microsoft Forms, meeting presenters can prepare, launch, and evaluate polls before, during, and after meetings, respectively, all from one place under a tab in the Teams meeting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-279">作为会议主持人，可以将 Forms 应用添加为 Teams 会议中的选项卡，然后从一个地方创建、发起和评估投票。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-279">As a meeting presenter, you can add the Forms app as a tab in the Teams meeting, then create, launch, and evaluate your polls from one place.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-280">创建要在会议期间甚至在会议开始之前发起的投票。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-280">Create polls to be launched during the meeting even before the meeting begins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-281">然后，结束会议后，可以选择在选项卡、导出的 Excel 工作簿中或在 Web 上的表单应用程序中评估回复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-281">Then, after the meeting, you can choose to evaluate responses in the tab, an exported Excel workbook, or on the web in the Forms app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-282">演示者拥有多种控件，例如启用匿名响应，关闭投票以及将结果导出到 Excel。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-282">Presenters have a variety of controls, like enabling anonymous responses, closing polls, and exporting results to Excel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-283">任何端点（移动、Web、桌面）的参与者都可以查看和回答会议屏幕或会议聊天中显示的投票，并实时查看非匿名投票结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-283">Attendees from any endpoint (mobile, web, desktop) can view and answer polls as they appear on the meeting screen or in the meeting chat, as well as see non-anonymous poll results in real time.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-284">**会议反应：** 会议反应是在会议中进行交互的新方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-284">**Meeting reactions:** Meeting reactions are a new way to interact in meetings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-285">参与者可以发送反应，并且这些反应将以流的形式显示在共享内容以及发送响应的个人上（如果它们在会议阶段显示）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-285">Participants can send reactions and they'll be shown as a stream on content that is shared, and on the individual who sent the reaction if they're displayed on the meeting stage.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-286">**桌面客户端历史记录菜单：** Teams桌面客户端中的“历史记录菜单”可让你轻松返回最近访问的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-286">**History Menu for desktop client:** The History Menu in Teams desktop client lets you easily get back to recently visited locations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-287">只需将鼠标悬停在桌面客户端中的前进或后退导航选项上，然后选择位置即可。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-287">Simply hover over the forward or backward navigation options in the desktop client and select the location.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-288">也可使用键盘快捷方式打开菜单。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-288">A keyboard shortcut is also available to open the menu.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-289">**Microsoft Teams 会议室中的 Cortana** Microsoft Teams 会议室中的 Cortana 语音有助于从会议室拨打电话、加入或结束会议或向会议添加电话号码时拥有非接触式体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-289">**Cortana in Microsoft Teams Rooms for US:** Cortana voice assistance in Microsoft Teams Rooms lets you have a touchless experience for calling a number from your conference room, joining or ending a meeting, or adding a number to a meeting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-290">**屏蔽电话号码：** 我们发布了新的管理员设置，可在拨入者加入会议时向他们屏蔽电话号码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-290">**Masking phone numbers:** We released a new admin setting for masking phone numbers for dial-in participants when they join a meeting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-291">管理员可以选择仅向外部人员屏蔽会议中的每个人（组织者除外）的电话号码，或禁用屏蔽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-291">Admins can choose to mask phone numbers from everyone in the meeting (except the organizer), from external people only or have masking disabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-292">如果管理员选择禁用此设置，则电话号码将在会议中完整显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-292">If the admins choose to have this setting disabled, the phone numbers will be displayed fully in the meeting.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-293">（十月底前专用版本）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-293">(private release until the end of October)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-294">**日历共享：** 新增了将频道添加到日历标签的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-294">**Calendar sharing:** We added the ability to add a channel to a calendar tab.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-295">**将更多场景引入同框场景模式：** Teams 现在已经为会议组织者或演示者引入了更改“同框场景模式”场景的功能，使参加者可以一起出现在不同的体验中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-295">**Bringing more scenes to Together Mode:** Teams have now introduced the ability for meeting organisers or presenters to change the Together Mode scene allowing attendees to appear in different experiences together.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-343">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-343">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-344">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-344">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-345">**将有关敏感度标签的​​审核数据发送给 M365 管理员：** 用户在文档和电子邮件上应用、更改或删除敏感度标签时，Office 会将审核数据发送到 M365 审核后端，供管理员查看。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-345">**Send audit data about sensitivity labeling to M365 administrators:** When users apply, change, or remove sensitivity labels on their documents and emails, Office will send up audit data to the M365 audit backend for administrators to see.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-346">这是一项静默功能（无 UI ），可让管理员受益。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-346">This is a silent functionality (no UI) for administrator benefit.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-347">**政府客户：对文档和电子邮件应用敏感度标签：** 敏感度标签功能现已适用于 GCC 和 GCC-H 环境中的客户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-347">**Government customers: Apply sensitivity labels to your documents and emails:** Sensitivity labeling features are now available for customers in the GCC and GCC-H environments.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-348">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-348">Learn more</span></span>](/microsoft-365/compliance/sensitivity-labels)

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-349">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-349">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-350">**邮件所有者删除对话：** 此功能允许你通过邮件所有者删除对话。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-350">**Delete conversation by message owner:** This feature allows you to delete a conversation by message owner.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-351">**在连续召开的会议之间提供时间：** 默认将会议设置为推迟 5-10 分钟开始，让与会者有时间喘口气或来往于不同地点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-351">**Build in time between back-to-back meetings:** Give attendees time to catch their breath or travel between locations by setting meetings to start 5-10 min late by default.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-352">了解详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-352">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/be84396a-0903-4e25-b31c-1c99ce0dacf2)

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-353">**所有联机会议：** 更新日历设置，确保在创建每个会议时都默认创建 Teams 会议，从而无需再记住单击“Teams 会议”选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-353">**Every meeting online:** Update your calendar settings to make every meeting you create a Teams Meeting by default so you no longer need to remember to click the Teams Meeting option.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-354">**将有关敏感度标签的​​审核数据发送给 M365 管理员：** 用户在文档和电子邮件上应用、更改或删除敏感度标签时，Office 会将审核数据发送到 M365 审核后端，供管理员查看。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-354">**Send audit data about sensitivity labeling to M365 administrators:** When users apply, change, or remove sensitivity labels on their documents and emails, Office will send up audit data to the M365 audit backend for administrators to see.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-355">这是一项静默功能（无 UI ），可让管理员受益。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-355">This is a silent functionality (no UI) for administrator benefit.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-356">**政府客户：对文档和电子邮件应用敏感度标签：** 敏感度标签功能现已适用于 GCC 和 GCC-H 环境中的客户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-356">**Government customers: Apply sensitivity labels to your documents and emails:** Sensitivity labeling features are now available for customers in the GCC and GCC-H environments.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-357">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-357">Learn more</span></span>](/microsoft-365/compliance/sensitivity-labels)

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-534">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-534">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-535">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-535">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-536">我们修复了在发送任务状态报告时导致“收件人”字段为空的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-536">We fixed an issue that caused the To field to be blank when sending a status report on a task.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-537">我们修复了导致 MailItem.BeforeAttachmentAdd 事件被破坏的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-537">We fixed an issue that caused the MailItem.BeforeAttachmentAdd event to be broken.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-538">我们添加了一个 regkey，允许客户在 IDataObject 操作中禁用附件的 filetime 包含（例如，拖放、剪贴板）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-538">We added a regkey that allows customers to disable filetime inclusion for attachments in IDataObject operations (i.e. drag drop, clipboard).</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-539">HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\Attachments。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-539">HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\Attachments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-540">REG_DWORD IncludeFileTimesInDataObject。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-540">REG_DWORD IncludeFileTimesInDataObject.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-541">0 = filetimes 被排除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-541">0 = filetimes are excluded.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-542">1 = （默认）包含 filetime。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-542">1 = (default) filetimes are included.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-543">我们修复了以下问题：当回复带有来自 Azure 信息保护的保护标签的邮件时，将导致嵌入式图像消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-543">We fixed an issue that caused inline images to disappear when replying to a message with a protection label from Azure Information Protection.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-547">修复了一些损坏的 PowerPoint 文件无法正常打开（即使在执行文档修复操作后也是如此）的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-547">Fixed an issue where some corrupt PowerPoint files were not opening correctly, even after a document repair operation.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-584">**跟上时代!日期/时间扩展数据类型具有更好的精度 。:** 引入新的改进的数据类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-584">**Keep up with the times! The Date/Time Extended data type has better precision.:** Introducing a new and improved data type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-585">为了增强与SQL的语法兼容性，并提高包含日期和时间的记录的准确性和详细程度，我们将DateTime2数据类型实现到Access中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-585">To enhance syntax compatibility with SQL, and to increase accuracy and level of detail in records that include dates and times, we’re implementing the DateTime2 data type into Access.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-586">这个额外的日期和时间数据类型将包括更大的日期范围(0001-01-01通过 9999-12-31)，具有更高的指定时间精度(使用纳秒，而不是秒)，你将能够提供和执行计算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-586">This additional date & time data type will include a larger date range (0001-01-01 through 9999-12-31), with higher-specified time precision (nanoseconds, rather than seconds) that you will be able to provide and perform calculations on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-587">要启用，请选择新字段> Date & Time Extended。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-587">To enable, select New field > Date & Time Extended.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-588">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-588">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/708c32da-a052-4cc2-9850-9851042e0024)

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-630">修复了导致 Outlook 为已启用云设置的用户创建第二个空签名的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-630">We fixed an issue that caused Outlook to create a second empty signature for people who had cloud settings enabled.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-719">修复了以下问题：在冻结工作表首行后使用快速分析时，Excel 可能会崩溃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-719">Fixed an issue where Excel could crash when using the Quick Analysis after freezing the top row of the sheet.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-720">修复了以下问题：如果工作簿包含使用 IFNA() 的公式，则可能导致有关损坏的工作簿的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-720">Fixed an issue that could cause a warning about a corrupt workbook if it contained formulas using IFNA().</span></span>

### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-773">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-773">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-774">**呼叫合并：**“呼叫合并”使最终用户能够将其现行的未保持 1 对 1 呼叫合并到另一个 1 对 1 呼叫或另一个组呼叫中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-774">**Call Merge:** Call Merge gives end users the capability to merge their active unheld 1-1 call into another 1-1 call or another group call.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-775">这适用于 Teams VOIP 呼叫和 PSTN 呼叫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-775">This applies to Teams VOIP calls and PSTN calls.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-776">**管理员可以为其一线工作人员配置基于班次的状态（上班、下班）：** 管理员可以将其一线工作人员配置为具有基于班次的状态：上班、忙碌（上班时可以切换）和下班。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-776">**Admins can configure shift-based presence (On shift, Off shift) for their Firstline workers:** Admins can configure their firstline workers to have shift-based presence states: On shift, Busy (can be toggled when on shift), and Off shift.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-777">**Teams 中的 Cortana 语音技能：** Teams 移动应用中的 Cortana 语音技能可帮助用户仅使用自然语言执行会议、交流和协作任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-777">**Cortana voice skills in Teams:** Cortana voice skills in Teams mobile app help users perform meeting, communication and collaboration tasks simply using spoken natural language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-778">用户可以通过在 Teams 应用中单击麦克风按钮来与 Cortana 对话，如果他们需要在做家务、遛狗或者忙个不停时与他人联系，可以通过该应用来发出“打电话给 Megan”或“给我的下一个会议发消息”等请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-778">Users can speak to Cortana by clicking on the microphone button in Teams app and make requests like “Call Megan” or “Send a message to my next meeting” if they need to connect with someone while juggling household chores or walking the dog or generally on the go.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-779">用户只需说“加入我的下一个会议”即可加入会议，或者通过询问“今天早上有哪些工作”来查看日历。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-779">Users can join meetings simply by saying “Join my next meeting” or check their calendar by asking “what do I have this morning”.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-780">在会议或呼叫中，他们可以在会议阶段从溢出菜单中调用 Cortana，并执行典型的会议中任务，例如按姓名或电话号码添加人员（“将 Megan 添加到呼叫”）、幻灯片组演示（“显示季度回顾幻灯片组”）或浏览幻灯片（“转到附录幻灯片”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-780">Once in a meeting or a call, they can invoke Cortana from the overflow menu in the meeting stage and perform typical in-meeting tasks like adding people by name or number (“Add Megan to the call”), deck presentation (“present the quarterly review deck”) or navigating slides (“Go to the appendix slide”).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-781">该功能还支持查找和共享文件、搜索以及在 Teams 应用中进行常规导航（与 John 聊天、转到未读活动、转到我的 @提及等）等事务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-781">Other things that the feature supports are finding and sharing files, search, and generally navigating within the Teams app (“Open my chat with John, Go to my unread activity, Go to my mentions etc.).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-782">Teams 中的 Cortana 满足[在线服务条款 (OST)](https://www.microsoft.com/licensing/product-licensing/products)中反映的对 Cortana 企业服务的企业级隐私、安全性和合规性承诺。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-782">Cortana in Teams meets the same enterprise-level privacy, security, and compliance promises for Cortana enterprise services, as reflected in the [Online Services Terms (OST)](https://www.microsoft.com/licensing/product-licensing/products).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-783">**群聊功能增加：** Teams 新增了一项功能，可以进行 250 位参与者的群聊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-783">**Group chat increase:** Teams added the ability to now have 250 participants in a group chat.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-784">**按班次标记：** 通过此功能，将自动为人员分配标记，与他们在 Teams 的 [Shifts 应用](https://support.microsoft.com/office/get-started-in-shifts-5f3e30d8-1821-4904-be26-c3cd25a497d6#bkmk_openshiftsappdesktop)中的日程安排和班次组名称相匹配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-784">**Tagging by Shift:** With this feature, people are automatically assigned tags that match their schedule and shift group name in the [Shifts app](https://support.microsoft.com/office/get-started-in-shifts-5f3e30d8-1821-4904-be26-c3cd25a497d6#bkmk_openshiftsappdesktop) in Teams.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-800">这个问题已经得到解决 - 现在，你可以在 Office 的即点即用应用程序之外使用我们的 ODBC 驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-800">This issue has been resolved - you can now use our ODBC driver outside of Office's Click-to-Run applications.</span></span>


### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-801">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-801">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-802">修复了导致尝试从添加到其个人资料的辅助帐户创建会议请求的用户看不到空白的“发件人：”字段，而是看到自己的电子邮件地址的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-802">Fixes an issue that caused users who attempted to create a meeting request from a secondary account added to their profile to not see a blank From: field instead of their email address.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-803">修复了导致用户无法在添加共享邮箱后连接到公用文件夹的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-803">Fixes an issue that caused users to be unable to connect to Public Folders after adding a shared mailbox.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-804">解决了导致在某些情况下，无法在代理拒绝会议时将其从经理的日历中删除的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-804">Addressed an issue that caused meetings to fail to be removed from a manager's calendar when declined by a delegate in some circumstances.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-805">解决了共享日历改进功能的部分用户无法查看新添加的共享日历的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-805">Addressed an issue that prevented some users of the Shared Calendar Improvements feature from being able to view a newly-added shared calendar.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-806">修复了导致用户在与云附件交互时偶尔出现崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-806">Fixes an issue that caused users to experience occasional crashes when interacting with Cloud attachments.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-807">解决了导致某些字符集的用户在向 SharePoint 文件添加智能链接时无法正确显示文件名的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-807">Addressed an issue that caused users of some character sets to see file names display incorrectly when adding a Smart Link to a SharePoint file.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-808">解决了导致用户在答复或撰写新的电子邮件时出现崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-808">Addresses an issue that caused users to experience a crash when replying to or composing new email.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-809">解决了通过选中 "仅下载邮件头" 选项删除来自 POP 帐户的4个或更多电子邮件时导致用户遇到崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-809">Addressed an issue which caused users to experience a crash when deleting 4 or more emails from a POP account with the "Download Headers Only" option selected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-810">解决了导致“日程安排助理”页面无法显示的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-810">Addressed an issue that caused some users to see the Scheduling Assistant page fail to display.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-811">修复了导致用户在编辑收件人时偶尔出现崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-811">This fixes an issue that caused users to experience occasional crashes when editing recipients.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-812">修复了导致用户在使用压缩视图时出现异常的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-812">Fixes an issue that caused users to see anomalies when using the compact view.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-813">解决了导致右键单击上下文菜单无法在搜索控件中显示的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-813">Addressed an issue that caused the right-click context menu to fail to appear in the search controls.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-814">解决了导致用户在答复或撰写新的电子邮件时收到错误的问题，其中该错误显示“此网页中的部分文件不在预期位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-814">Addresses an issue that caused users to receive the following error when replying to or composing new email, "Some of the files in this web page aren't in the expected location.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-815">是否仍要下载它们？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-815">Do you want to download them anyway?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-816">如果确定此网页来自可靠来源，请单击‘是’”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-816">If you’re sure the Web page is from a trusted source, click Yes"</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-860">**建立 PDF 连接：** 连接到 PDF，从其中导入数据，刷新数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-860">**Make a PDF connection:** Connect to, import, refresh data from a PDF.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-861">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-861">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/be4330b3-5356-486c-a168-b68e9e616f5a)

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-862">**不干扰他人筛选和排序：** 现在可以使用工作表视图与他人协作时排序和筛选你的 Excel 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-862">**Filter and sort without disrupting others:** You can now sort and filter your Excel file while collaborating with others with Sheet View.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-863">此新增功能可防止你在共同创作文档时受到其他用户的排序和筛选的影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-863">This new feature prevents you from being impacted by other user’s sorts and filters while coauthoring the document.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-864">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-864">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/0eea3dc5-d7d1-44c5-a953-25ebfbd6c1a6)

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-866">**在 Excel 中从 Power BI 中的数据集创建数据透视表：** 你可以在 Excel 中创建连接到 Power BI 中存储的数据集的数据透视表，只需点击几下鼠标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-866">**Create PivotTables from Datasets in Power BI within Excel:** You can create PivotTables in Excel that are connected to datasets stored in Power BI with a few clicks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-867">这样做可以让你更好地利用数据透视表和 Power BI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-867">Doing this allows you get the best of both PivotTables and Power BI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-868">使用数据透视表从你的安全的 Power BI 数据集计算、总结和分析数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-868">Calculate, summarize, and analyze your data with PivotTables from your secure Power BI datasets.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-869">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-869">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/31444a04-9c38-4dd7-9a45-22848c666884)<br /><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-870">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/06/11/use-power-bi-data-in-excel/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-870">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/06/11/use-power-bi-data-in-excel/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-885">**建议的答复：** 我们为 Teams 用户增加了对他们的对话提出建议答复的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-885">**Suggested replies:** We added the ability for Teams users to have a suggested reply to their conversations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-886">如果启用这些建议，它们将显示在聊天消息的底部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-886">These suggestions will appear at the bottom of a chat message if they are enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-887">他们使回复消息变得快速而轻松！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-887">They make replying to messages quick and easy!</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-888">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-888">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-889">**自动应用或推荐敏感度标签：** Office 可以根据检测到的敏感内容来推荐或自动应用敏感度标签。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-889">**Auto-apply or recommend sensitivity labels:** Office can recommend or automatically apply a sensitivity label based on the sensitive content detected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-890">**在矢量中保留文本：** 现在，在 Excel、Word 和 PowerPoint 中转换这些对象时，可以在地图、图表和其他SVG矢量中保留文本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-890">**Retain text in vectors:** Now you can retain the text in maps, charts, and other SVG vectors when converting these objects in Excel, Word, and PowerPoint.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-948">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-948">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-949">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-949">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-950">**更长文件名：** Windows 桌面版 Excel 现在支持名称和路径长达 400 字符的 OneDrive/SharePoint 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-950">**Longer file names:** Excel for Windows desktop now supports OneDrive/SharePoint files with names and paths of up to 400 characters.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-951">**Realtimedata (RTD) 改进：** 在 Office 365 版本 2002 每月频道或更高版本中，Excel 的 RealTimeData (RTD) 函数要比 Excel 2010 计算电子表格中的数据的速度快得多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-951">**Realtimedata (RTD) improvements:** In Office 365 version 2002 monthly channel and later, Excel's RealTimeData (RTD) function is much faster than Excel 2010 calculating data in the spreadsheet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-952">我们在其基本内存和数据结构中删除瓶颈，并使其变得线程安全，这能允许其在 多线程计算 (MTR) 的所有可用线程上进行计算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-952">We removed bottlenecks in its underlying memory and data structures as well as made it thread-safe to allow  it to be calculated on all available threads of Multithreaded recalculation (MTR).</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-953">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-953">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-954">**新增了用于在 Outlook 中撰写邮件时禁用 @提及建议的选项：** 你是否觉得 @提及选取器更令人生厌，而不是更有用？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-954">**New option to disable @ mention suggestions when composing mail in Outlook:** Do you find the @ mention picker more annoying than useful?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-955">现在，可以根据需要禁用它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-955">Now you can turn it off if you prefer.</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-956">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/03/26/feedback-in-action-disable-mentions/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-956">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/03/26/feedback-in-action-disable-mentions/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-959">**在 Outlook toast 通知中增加了额外的按钮：** 在 Windows 10 上运行 Outlook 时，Outlook toast 通知中会出现快速操作按钮</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-959">**Additional buttons added to Outlook toast notifications:** Quick Action buttons now appear in Outlook toast notifications when running Outlook on Windows 10</span></span>

### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-963">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-963">Teams</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-967">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-967">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1060">**演示时同步所做的更改：** 即使演示文稿处于幻灯片放映模式，只要进行了更改就同步这些更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1060">**Synchronize changes while you are presenting:** Synchronize changes whenever they are made even when the presentation is in slide show mode.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1061">了解更多详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1061">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/5a2921a9-97d4-436b-b0cd-295dfe2236bb)<br /><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1062">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/04/08/synchronize-changes-while-presenting/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1062">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/04/08/synchronize-changes-while-presenting/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1063">**无需遥控器：使用耳塞即可：** 使用 Surface Earbuds 来控制 PowerPoint 演示文稿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1063">**No need for a clicker: your earbuds have you covered:** Use your Surface Earbuds to control your PowerPoint presentations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1064">工作原理：配对后，需要在 PowerPoint 中启用此功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1064">How it works:  Once paired, you'll need to enable the feature in PowerPoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1065">通过按 F5 或选择“幻灯片放映” > “从头开始”开始演示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1065">Start a presentation by pressing F5 or selecting Slide Show > From Beginning.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1066">在幻灯片放映中，右键单击幻灯片，然后在“ Surface Earbuds 设置”下选择“使用手势控制演示”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1066">In Slide Show, right click on the slide and under Surface Earbuds Settings choose Use Gestures to Control Presentation.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1067">在以后的所有演示中都会记住此设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1067">This setting will be remembered for all future presentations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1068">现在可以在左侧耳机上向前向后滑动，以在幻灯片放映模式中浏览演示文稿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1068">You can now can swipe forward and backward on the left earbud to navigate your presentations in Slide Show mode.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1069">双击播放或暂停嵌入视频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1069">Double tap to play or pause embedded videos.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1070">重要提示：必须使用 Windows 10 的 Surface Audio 应用配对 Surface Earbuds，才能使用手势控制演示文稿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span ### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1073">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1073">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1074">**更换为 Teams 会议中的视频版式：** 很快，在 Teams 会议中可以同时查看的与会人员将从 4 人增加到 9 人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1074">**Changes to video layout in Teams meetings:** Soon, the number of participants that can be viewed simultaneously during a Teams meeting will increase from 4 to 9.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1075">**直播活动中包含音频系统：** 现在，直播活动中的演示者和制作人可以在直播活动中共享桌面或窗口屏幕时包括系统音频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1075">**Include system audio in live events:** Presenters and producers in live events can now include system audio when sharing a desktop or window screen during the live event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1076">这将使您的用户听到所共享内容的任何音频部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1076">This will allow your users to hear any audio part of the content you are sharing.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1077">**使组织者能够更改拨号参与者的会议厅设置：** 此设置控制通过电话拨入的用户是否直接加入会议或在大厅中等待，无需考虑 “自动允许人员” 设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1077">**Enable organizers to change lobby settings for dial-in participants:** This setting controls whether people who dial in by phone join the meeting directly or wait in the lobby regardless of the Automatically admit people setting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1078">**在会议中举手：** 用户现在可以在会议中举起虚拟手！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1078">**Raise Your Hand in Meetings:** Users can now raise a virtual hand in a meeting!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1079">其他与会者将在会议台的姓名旁或名册的姓名旁看到你举起的手。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1079">Other participants will see your raised hand next to your name in the meeting stage and next to your name in the roster.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1080">**自定义会议视频背景：** 使用视频会议时，现可选择不同的静态背景图像。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1080">**Customize meeting video backgrounds:** When you are meeting with video, you now have the choice of different static background images to use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1081">这将让你显示此图像，而不是你所坐位置的实际背景。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1081">This will let you show this image and not the actual background of where you are sitting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1082">**添加更多人员至聊天：** 现在，我们可以在一个聊天线程中最多添加 350 人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1082">**Add more people to chat:** We made it possible to now add up to 350 people to a single chat thread.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1083">**活动源“设置”齿轮：** 用户现在可以通过设置齿轮直接从源左栏访问活动源和通知设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1083">**Settings Gear on your Activity Feed:** Users can now directly access activity feed and notification setting from the feed left rail by the means of a settings gear.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1084">**轻松从进行中的 Teams 会议访问选项：** Teams 会议开始后，我们通过直接在参与者窗格中提供易于访问的链接，使会议组织者更快、轻松地更改其演示者和会议厅设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1084">**Easily access meeting options from within a Teams meeting in progress:** We are making it easier for meeting organizers to quickly and easily change their presenter and lobby settings once a Teams meeting starts by providing an easy to access link directly in the participants pane.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1085">此新功能将同时出现在预定会议和“立即开会”会议中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1085">This new functionality will be present for both scheduled and “Meet Now” meetings.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1086">**团队和频道分析：** 除团队分析之外，现在还可以查看频道级别的指标和见解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1086">**Team and channel analytics:** In addition to team analytics, now you can also view channel level metrics and insights.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1087">我们还将时间范围延长到 90 天，因此可以分析更长的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1087">We've also enhanced the time period to 90 days so you can analyze data for longer periods.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1088">除此之外，此版本还包括有关团队或渠道的文章、回复和会议数量的新指标和图表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1088">Apart from that, this release also includes new metrics and charts around count of posts, replies and meetings for a team or channel.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1089">**进入/退出公告：** 我们添加了此功能，使会议组织者可以打开或关闭进入和退出会议的公告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1089">**Entry/exit announcements:** We added this feature that lets meeting organizers have the ability to turn on or off entry and exit announcements for a meeting.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1090">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1090">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1091">**无需退出 Word 即可解码首字母缩写词：** 遇到首字母缩写词时，Word 将会根据其他人的使用情况定义它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1091">**Decode acronyms without leaving Word:** When you encounter an acronym, Word will try to define it based on how others use it.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1092">**使用动态 Gif 讲述故事：** 现在，Office 编辑器支持动画 Gif，你的文档更漂亮</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1092">**Tell your stories with animated GIFs:** Animated GIFs are now supported in the Office editor - your documents just got snazzier</span></span>

### <a name="skype"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1104">Skype</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1104">Skype</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1105">当用户被告知只能使用团队的策略时，他们仍然可以使用Skype for Business Outlook 插件来安排会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1105">When a user is given a policy that moves them to Teams Only, they were still able to use the Skype for Business Outlook add-in to schedule meetings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1106">在此更新之后，当客户端读取指示用户为仅限团队的策略并进入仅限会议加入模式后，你将不再能够为Skype安排商务会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1106">After this update, you will no longer be able to schedule Skype for Business meetings after the client reads the policy indicating the user is Teams Only, and enters meeting join only mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1107">另外，如果 Skype for Business Outlook 插件在启动时看到 Skype for Business客户端处于会议加入模式，它将不会激活自己。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1107">Additionally the Skype for Business Outlook Add-in will not activate itself while starting up if it sees the Skype for Business client is in meeting join only mode.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1108">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1108">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1109">此更新修复了 Microsoft Office 中 Visual Basic for Applications 的以下问题：某些引用库名称或库路径中包含 DBSC 字符的代码库的 VBA 项目会被 Office 应用程序视为加载时损坏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1109">This update fixes an issue in Visual Basic for Applications in Microsoft Office where certain VBA projects that contain references to code libraries with DBCS characters in the library name or library path would be viewed by the Office application as corrupt on load.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1110">此更新修复了 Microsoft Office 中的一个问题，即在运行时可能无法正确找到所含引用可通过搜索 PATH 环境变量中指定的位置找到的 Visual Basic for Applications 项目，从而导致 VBA 运行时错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1110">This update fixes an issue in Microsoft Office where Visual Basic for Applications projects with references that are expected to be found by searching locations specified in the PATH environment variable may not be found properly at runtime, leading to VBA runtime errors.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1111">当注册表键HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth被设置为零时，正在激活一个外接程序时，windows中的office主机故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1111">The office host was crashing in windows, when an add-in is being activated while the registry key HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth is set to zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1112">此更改可修复此问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1112">This change would fix this issue.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1138">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1138">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1139">此更新修复了 Microsoft Office 中 Visual Basic for Applications 的以下问题：某些引用库名称或库路径中包含 DBSC 字符的代码库的 VBA 项目会被 Office 应用程序视为加载时损坏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1139">This update fixes an issue in Visual Basic for Applications in Microsoft Office where certain VBA projects that contain references to code libraries with DBCS characters in the library name or library path would be viewed by the Office application as corrupt on load.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1230">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1230">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1231">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1231">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1232">**你喜爱的 Excel 函数运行速度更快：** SUMIFS、AVERAGEIFS、COUNTIFS、MAXIFS 和 MINIFS 函数运行速度比以往更快。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1232">**Your favorite Excel functions just got faster:** The SUMIFS, AVERAGEIFS, COUNTIFS, MAXIFS, and MINIFS functions are much faster than ever before.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1233">更快达到底线。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1233">Get to the bottom line more quickly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1234">立即试用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1234">Try one now.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1235">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1235">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1236">**将电子邮件拖动到你拥有的组：** 通过从收件箱中拖动来移动和复制邮件和对话。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1236">**Drag email to a group you own:** Move and copy messages and conversations by dragging them from your inbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1237">将与所有组成员共享你拖动的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1237">Messages you drag will be shared with all group members.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1238">**强制 wifi 网络新体验：** 是否已加入需要使用网页登录的 wifi 网络？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1238">**New experience for captive wifi networks:** Have you ever joined a wifi network that required a web page to sign in with?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1239">现在，Outlook 检测到这一点，帮助你进行连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1239">Outlook now detects this and helps you get connected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1257">通过临时调整 OneNote 2016 中的同步频率，提升了同步和服务稳定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1257">Improved sync and service stability by temporarily adjusting sync frequency in OneNote 2016.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1333">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1333">Feature updates</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1335">**随时随地阅读和答复：** 无需打开工作簿即可直接从电子邮件响应评论和提及。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1335">**Read and reply on the fly:** Respond to comments and mentions right from email without opening the workbook.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1336">**向左看，向右看… XLOOKUP 在此！** 使用 XLOOKUP 在表或区域中逐行查找所需内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1336">**Look left, look right… XLOOKUP is here!:** Row by row, find anything you need in a table or range with XLOOKUP.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1337">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1337">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/b7fd680e-6d10-43e6-84f9-88eae8bf5929)

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1338">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1338">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1339">**高级组电子邮件设置：** 此功能可帮助组用户自定义要在收件箱中接收/关注的电子邮件或事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1339">**Advanced group email settings:** This feature helps groups users to customize which emails or events to receive/follow in their inbox.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1340">**组命名策略：** 组命名策略使 IT 管理员能够标准化管理组织中由用户创建的组名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1340">**Groups Naming policy:** A group naming policy enables the IT admin to standardize and manage the names of groups created by users in the organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1341">管理员可以要求在创建组时向名称添加特定前缀和后缀，并阻止使用指定的字词。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1341">The admin can require a specific prefix and suffix be added to the name for a group when it's created, and can block specific words from being used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1342">这有助于尽可能在组名中减少使用不适宜的字词，以及有助于IT部门在目录中管理组的显示方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1342">This helps minimize the use of inappropriate words in group names as well as IT manage the representation of groups in their directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1343">命名策略还可有助于组织根据部门部署团队网站，以进行分类。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1343">Naming Policy also helps organizations that deploy team sites to categorize them based on department.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1386">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1386">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1387">此更改通过利用软件呈现避免了某些 Intel 图形驱动程序的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1387">This change circumvents a problem with certain Intel graphics drivers by leveraging software rendering.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1388">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1388">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1389">解决了导致会议位置在清除后意外添加回会议的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1389">Addressed an issue that caused the location of a meeting to get added back to the meeting unexpectedly after clearing it.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1390">解决了导致用户在通过键盘快捷方式与其邮箱文件夹交互时出现明显延迟的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1390">Addressed an issue that caused users to see a noticeable delay when interacting with their mailbox folders through keyboard shortcuts.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1391">解决了在某些情况下导致用户看到电子邮件发送地址与显示的 SMTP 地址不匹配的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1391">Addressed an issue that caused users to see emails sent to an address that did not match the displayed SMTP address in some circumstances.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1392">解决了导致用户在检索云设置时在 Outlook 中遇到挂起的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1392">Addressed an issue that caused users to experience hangs in Outlook when retrieving Cloud Settings.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1394">构建基块管理器可能显示无效的警报：“你已更改样式、构建基块”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1394">Building blocks organizer may display an invalid alert: "You have modified styles, building blocks".</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1395">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1395">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="01bdf-1396">解决了 Office 更新可能已意外地从 Office CDN 而不是计划源（例如本地/网络共享或 Configuration Manager 提供的位置）下载文件的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="01bdf-1396">Resolved an issue where Office updates may have unexpectedly downloaded files from the Office CDN instead of the intended source, such as a local or network share, or Configuration Manager-provided location.</span></span>
